-- 주문 테이블 TB_ORDER 삭제
DROP TABLE TB_ORDER;

-- 주문 테이블 TB_ORDER 생성
CREATE TABLE "TB_ORDER" (
   "ORDER_NO" NUMBER NOT NULL,
   "USER_NO" NUMBER NOT NULL,
   "ORDER_DATE" DATE DEFAULT SYSDATE NULL,
   "POST" VARCHAR2(7) NOT NULL,
   "ADDRESS" VARCHAR2(100) NOT NULL,
   "ADDRESS_DETAIL" VARCHAR2(300) NOT NULL,
   "RECEIVER" VARCHAR2(15) NOT NULL,
   "PHONE"   VARCHAR2(13) NOT NULL,
    -- 결제 번호 UNIQUE 제약조건 추가
   "PAYMENT_NO" NUMBER   NOT NULL UNIQUE,
   "PAYMENT_TYPE" VARCHAR2(30)   NOT NULL,
   "PAYMENT_STATUS" NUMBER   NULL,	
   "ORDER_MESSAGE"   VARCHAR2(100) NULL,
   "TOTAL_AMOUNT" NUMBER NULL,
   "POINT_USE"   NUMBER NULL,
    -- CHECK제약조건추가
    CHECK(PAYMENT_TYPE IN ('카드', '은행', '무통장입금', '간편결제')),
    CHECK(PAYMENT_STATUS IN (0, 1))
);
COMMIT;

-- 시퀀스 삭제
DROP SEQUENCE SEQ_ONO;

-- 시퀀스 생성
CREATE SEQUENCE SEQ_ONO
  START WITH 1
  INCREMENT BY 1
  NOMAXVALUE;
